246001954 Let's see...mainly this gets rid of FastImages and Images and replaces them with FGS with different scores. In the interface, FGS and IMaGES are only distinguished in that FGS takes a single data set, covariance matrix, or graph as input, whereas IMaGES can take those plus multiple data sets/covariance matrices as input. GES is eliminated from the interface (and probably will be eliminated from the code). BDeu score is still being negotiated.
